***искрививший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:искривить.html>искриви́вший</a> (17916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искривить.html>искриви́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iskrivívšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искривить.html>искриви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iskrivítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:искривить.html>искриви́вший</a></b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">is-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кривить.html>криви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krivítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искривить.html>искриви́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iskrivítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">искривля́ть</b>)

<li>to distort</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***искриться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:искриться.html>искри́ться</a> (11595)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искра.html>и́скра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ískra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (stem-stressed variant) or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искра.html>и́скра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ískra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (ending-stressed variant).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искриться.html>и́скриться</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искриться.html>искри́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ískritʹsja</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iskrítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заи́скриться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заискри́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spark</li>
<li>to sparkle, to effervesce, to fizz</li>
<li>to scintillate</li>
<li>to glisten</li>
<li>to glister</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ис<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>кри́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — заискриться.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:альтернативный.html>альтернати́вный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> спряжения (<a href = vnd.unilang:анализировать.html>инфинитив</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:искриться.html>и́скриться</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ма</a> спряжения 4a). 
</p>

***искупить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:искупить.html>искупи́ть</a> (16198)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">is-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искупить.html>искупи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iskupítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искупать.html>искупа́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:искус.html>искус</a> (30913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">искусъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iskusŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искус.html>и́скус</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искус.html>иску́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ískus</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iskús</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искус.html>и́скуса</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искус.html>иску́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искус.html>и́скусы</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искус.html>иску́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искус.html>и́скусов</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искус.html>иску́сов</a></b>)

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:искусный.html>иску́сно</a> (12580)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искусный.html>иску́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iskúsnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искусный.html>иску́сно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iskúsno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ably, skillfully <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">with great ability</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искусный.html>иску́сно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iskúsno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искусный.html>иску́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iskúsnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***искусный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:искусный.html>иску́сный</a> (11821)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">искуси́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iskusítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искусный.html>иску́сный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iskúsnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>skillful, skilled, crafty
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:искусный.html>иску́сная</a></b> рукоде́льница.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná <b>iskúsnaja</b> rukodélʹnica.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She is clever with her needle.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ис<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ку́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>сный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>иску́снее.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-искусн-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***искусственный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:искусственный.html>иску́сственный</a> (3069)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iskússtvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искусственный.html>иску́сственный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iskússtvennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>artificial, man-made
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свеча.html>све́чи</a> - <b><a href = vnd.unilang:искусственный.html>иску́сственные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:источник.html>исто́чники</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Svéči - <b>iskússtvennyje</b> istóčniki svéta.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Candles are <b>artificial</b> light sources.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dentistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> false <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in terms of teeth</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>imitation, fake</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unnatural, insincere, contrived</li></ol>

***искусство.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сство</a> (997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">искусьство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iskusĭstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">искоусъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iskusŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">test, experiment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, likely from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kustiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">choice, trail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵews-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">choice</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gusto</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iskússtvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>art</li>
<li>skill, craftsmanship, craft</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:искушать.html>искуша́ть</a> (20300)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">искуси́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iskusítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:искушать.html>искуша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iskušátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">искуси́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to experience, to acquire knowledge of</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to test, to tempt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:искушать.html>искуша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>судьбу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>iskušátʹ</b> sudʹbú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tempt fate</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tempt, to entice, to seduce</li></ol>

***исламский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:исламский.html>исла́мский</a> (14926)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">испари́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isparítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испарение.html>испаре́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">isparénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испарение.html>испаре́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испарение.html>испаре́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испарение.html>испаре́ний</a></b>)

***испариться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:испариться.html>испари́ться</a> (13077)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">испари́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isparítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испариться.html>испари́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">isparítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испаряться.html>испаря́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to evaporate, to vaporize, to turn into vapor</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disappear, to vanish into thin air</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to walk; to be stolen</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">испари́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isparítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sense 2</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потеряться.html>потеря́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poterjátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sense 3</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">plural</span><span class="ib-comma">,</span> past tense</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> вы́несенны</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">býli výnesenny</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ис<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:па.html>па</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ри́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
